\begin{document}
\maketitle
\noindent This file is the canonical, dated record of every change to the TFPT theory
development: new verification modules (\texttt{vN}), status changes, editorial passes and
infrastructure. It is maintained \emph{in the same change} as the work it records, and it is
also imported at the end of the \texttt{introduction} document. Module numbers \texttt{vN}
refer to \texttt{verification/vN\_*.py}; claim IDs refer to rows of
\texttt{verification/status\_ledger.csv}.
\fi

\ifdefined\ChangelogImported
\clearpage
\section*{Appendix: changelog}
\addcontentsline{toc}{section}{Appendix: changelog}
\noindent The dated record of every change (canonical source: \texttt{changelog.tex}, also
compiled standalone). Module numbers \texttt{vN} refer to \texttt{verification/vN\_*.py}.
\fi

\subsection*{2026-07-22 (IV) (external review integrated: route renamed, object diagram, group-extension definition, SEAM.EQUIV route split (MMST/TWISTOR ids, no status change), $A_3$ role table, \texttt{WOIT.OS.TWISTOR.01} contract --- a pure structure/text integration, NO new physics claims, NO marker moves, suite unchanged at $508$)}

missing. Six changes plus one new central research contract, all editorial/structural:

structure/boundary values), lists TFPT's existing ingredients (RP \texttt{v379}, OS reconstruction,

\subsection*{2026-06-30 (\texttt{v445} --- the rigidity FORCING converse: commuting with the order-$4$ clock is \emph{exactly} $\mu_4$-block-diagonality, upgrading the rigidity step from ``permit'' to ``force'')}

single remaining physical premise. \mE\ FORCING (entrywise iff): $[\rho,K]{=}0$ iff $K_{ij}{=}0$ whenever

$\mu_4$-block-diagonality, it does not merely permit it. \mE\ EXACT COMMUTANT DIMENSION:
$\dim\{K:[\rho,K]{=}0\}{=}\sum_s n_s^2$ (the $\mathrm{ad}_\rho$ nullspace), a proper subspace of the full $N^2$
algebra ($N{=}16$: $64{<}256$) --- a genuine quantitative restriction. \mE\ OFF-BLOCK $\Leftrightarrow$
NON-COMMUTING: every off-block matrix unit has $\|[\rho,E_{ij}]\|{\ge}\sqrt2{>}0$ (zero slack). \mE\ THE ORDER IS
THE DISCRIMINATOR: the order-$4$ clock gives $4$ sectors; the order-$2$ clock leaves a strictly larger commutant
($N{=}16$: $64$ vs $128$) --- the four Gauss--Bonnet marks (order $4{=}|\mu_4|{=}h(A_3)$) force strictly more
structure than two, and only the index-$4$ extension is $(E_8)_1$ ($\det{=}1$; \texttt{v281}/\texttt{v154}/\texttt{v351}).
\mE\ NONDEGENERACY: exactly $4$ distinct eigenvalues $\{1,i,-1,-i\}$ for all $N{\ge}4$. \mC\ SYNTHESIS: commuting
with the order-$4$ $\mu_4$ clock is \emph{equivalent} to $\mu_4$-block-diagonality, so RP-definability
(\texttt{v54}/\texttt{v398}) $+$ clock-invariance \emph{force} the block-diagonal $\Lambda_\Sigma$ ---

$JPJ{=}P_+$ (and $\operatorname{tr}K{=}0$). The cited Borchers/Wiesbrock theorem and the one continuum input
(the continuum standard pair) are named axioms; the composition pins face~(ii) of \texttt{SEAM.EQUIV.01} to
exactly those two --- intrinsic Bisognano--Wichmann, no rotation-covariance presupposed.

audit count, kernel-checked (hardens \texttt{v441}).} The headline bookkeeping is itself machine-verified: of
the $12$ cited-theorem hypotheses (MMST/NPW26/Adamo, mirrored in order) exactly $11$ are internal and $1$
external (\texttt{total\_count}=12, \texttt{internal\_count}=11, \texttt{external\_count}=1), plus

(pure kernel \texttt{decide}). The single external fact (continuum scaling-limit existence) is the named axiom;
the keystone reduction pins its external dependence to exactly that one fact.
\item \textbf{Net.} Both modules are imported by the root \texttt{TfptCarrier.lean}, axiom-audited in

\subsection*{2026-06-30 (shadow-export coherence --- the \texttt{tfpt5-shadow} mirror is now reproducible \emph{as shipped}: the audit is shadow-aware, the content maps are non-destructive on the website-free subset, and an export gate blocks any incoherent mirror)}
\begin{itemize}
\item \textbf{Context (reviewer finding, Alessandro).} On the exported \texttt{tfpt5\_shadow.zip}

Red Team; Lean transcript), but the \emph{package} layer did not: \texttt{make\_manifest.py --check}

unconditionally required \texttt{website/lib/release.ts}, which the shadow subset deliberately excludes.
\item \textbf{\texttt{make\_docs\_map.py} is now shadow-aware.} \texttt{website\_map.csv} mirrors the
\texttt{website/} sources; on a tree without \texttt{website/} the generator now \emph{skips} it instead of
regenerating it down to a single \texttt{README.md} row. This removes the silent corruption that made
\texttt{build.sh notes}/\texttt{gen} leave \texttt{website\_map.csv} stale against the manifest on the export
(it now matches the established skips in \texttt{make\_script\_index.py} and \texttt{make\_changelog\_web.py}).
\item \textbf{\texttt{audit\_sync.py} is now shadow-aware.} When \texttt{website/} is absent it skips the
website mirror (section D), the website version stamps (E) and the website Wolfram-count card (F), and the
website generated-surface freshness in (A), printing exactly which sections were skipped. \texttt{build.sh audit}
therefore runs to a clean \texttt{AUDIT OK} on the shadow subset instead of raising \texttt{FileNotFoundError}.
\item \textbf{Export coherence gate.} \texttt{scripts/export-shadow.sh} now re-runs
\texttt{make\_manifest.py --check} and the shadow-aware \texttt{audit\_sync.py} \emph{on the filtered tree}
before the mirror is published. The manifest check catches the earlier \texttt{v235--v298} symptom at the
source: a module referenced by \texttt{run\_all.py}/\texttt{script\_registry.csv}/\texttt{manifest.sha256} but
not committed (and thus dropped by \texttt{git ls-files}) now fails the export loudly instead of shipping a
package that says \texttt{ALL CHECKS PASSED} while \texttt{run\_all.py} stops at the first missing script.
\item \textbf{Manifest refreshed.} \texttt{manifest.sha256} was regenerated as the last release step so the
shipped digests match the committed \texttt{changelog.tex} and \texttt{website\_map.csv}; the full Python
suite reproduces end-to-end on the regenerated export. No theory content, status marker or \texttt{vN} module
changed --- this is an export/infrastructure fix only.
\end{itemize}

\subsection*{2026-06-29 (\texttt{v435} --- a fourth honest step on the $\ainv$ Quillen target: a $\pi$-power test isolates the cubic $\alpha^3$ as the unique metric-independent (topological) rung, and types its coefficient as a conditional integer level)}
\begin{itemize}
\item \textbf{New module \texttt{v435} (\texttt{ALPHA.QUILLEN.PROGRESS.04}) --- it attacks the \emph{single}
remaining \mO\ left after \vref{v434} (residual (2), the cubic $\alpha^3$ Chern/Maxwell moment) and
\emph{sharpens} it; it does \emph{not} close it.} The target \texttt{ALPHA.QUILLEN.EXACT.01} (\vref{v382})
stays \mO; $\ainv=137.0359992$ stays \mE.
\begin{itemize}
\item \mE\ \textbf{$\pi$-power / metric-independence test.} The three EM-closure coefficients carry
$\pi$-powers exactly $\{0,3,6\}$, equal to their $\cthree$-orders: Maxwell $k_0=1\to\pi^0$, Calder\'on
$-2\cthree^3=-1/(256\pi^3)\to\pi^3$, transport $-8b_1\cthree^6=-41/(327680\pi^6)\to\pi^6$. So the Maxwell
$a^3$ is the \emph{unique} $\pi^0/\cthree^0$ (metric-\emph{independent}) term. A heat-kernel boundary
coefficient always carries the $(4\pi)^{-d/2}$ measure; a metric-independent term carries none --- the
signature of a \emph{topological} term. The test thus partitions the closure into \emph{one} topological
level ($a^3$) $+$ \emph{two} heat-kernel boundary terms, confirming \vref{v342}/\vref{v434}'s ``$a^3$ is a
level, not a Seeley--DeWitt curvature integral'' from a \emph{test} rather than a claim.
\item \mC\ \textbf{conditional level quantisation.} \emph{If} the $a^3$ term is the seam $U(1)$
Chern--Simons/$\eta$ boundary level (the \texttt{EM1} reading, \vref{v48}), large-gauge invariance
quantises the level to $\Z$, so $k_0=1$ is the \emph{unit} (minimal) level --- an integer, not a tunable
real. This converts ``the coefficient happens to be $1$'' into ``the coefficient is an integer level and
$1$ is the unit''.
\item \mO\ \textbf{not closed:} the \texttt{EM1} lemma itself --- the from-first-principles Chern--Simons
boundary proof that $\partial_\tau\log Z_{\mathrm{Maxwell}}=a^3$ --- stays external math (type A, \vref{v384});
the seam $F$-normalisation stays the one \mC\ (residuals 1\,\&\,3, \vref{v434}); $\ainv$ stays \mE.
\end{itemize}
\item \textbf{Surfaces updated.} Registered in \texttt{run\_all.py}, \texttt{script\_registry.csv} and

subsection beside \vref{v433}/\vref{v434}; mirrored on the website residual-gap lab. Python-only; no new
physical number.
\end{itemize}

\subsection*{2026-06-28 (\texttt{v434} --- a third honest step on the $\ainv$ Quillen target: $b_1$ is the $a_4$ heat-kernel coefficient, and the three residuals collapse to one $\mathrm{[C]}$ $+$ one $\mathrm{[O]}$)}
\begin{itemize}
\item \textbf{New module \texttt{v434} (\texttt{ALPHA.QUILLEN.PROGRESS.03}) --- it settles the status of the
three residuals named after \vref{v433} and shows they are \emph{not} three independent open problems.} The
target \texttt{ALPHA.QUILLEN.EXACT.01} (\vref{v382}) stays \mO; $\ainv=137.0359992$ stays \mE.
\begin{itemize}
\item \mE\ \textbf{$b_1$ \emph{is} the $U(1)$ $a_4$ heat-kernel coefficient (the $\beta=a_4$ theorem).} The
one-loop $\beta$ function of a gauge coupling \emph{is} the $a_4$ (Seeley--DeWitt $a_2$ in $d{=}4$) heat-kernel
coefficient of the charged-field operator (Vassilevich). Computed from the carrier hypercharge content with the
standard spin weights ($\tfrac23$ per Weyl fermion, $\tfrac13$ per complex scalar),
$\sum\tfrac23 Y_f^2+\tfrac13 Y_s^2 = 41/6$ (SM) and $(3/5)\cdot{}$that $=41/10=b_1$ (GUT). So the $b_1$ in the
counterterm $8b_1\cthree^6$ is the $a_4$ coefficient of the carrier $U(1)_Y$ content (the same number as the
$\beta$, \vref{v159}/\vref{v246}), the \emph{same kind} of heat-kernel object as the $\alpha^2$ Calder\'on $a_4$
(\vref{v342}) --- not a fitted multiplicity.
\item \mE\ \textbf{the geometry factors off:} $8b_1\cthree^6=b_1\cdot(\operatorname{rank}E_8)\cdot\cthree^6$, with
$\operatorname{rank}E_8=8$ the $\chi{=}2$ seam boundary count (\vref{v216}) and $\cthree^6$ the six boundary
insertions (the $\pi$-power test, \vref{v342}).
\item \mC\ \textbf{residual (1) $\equiv$ residual (3).} With $b_1$ and the $\cthree$-powers heat-kernel-forced,
the only freedom left in the exact seam $a_4$ value is how the gauge curvature couples to the boundary measure ---
the seam $F$-normalisation. So ``the actual seam $a_4=8b_1\cthree^6$'' and ``the seam $F$-normalisation'' are
\emph{one} \mC\ obligation, not two.
\item \mE\ \textbf{residual (2) located (not closed):} the determinant-line variation factors
$a^3-2\cthree^3 a^2 = a^2(a-2\cthree^3)$; $a^2$ is the Gilkey gauge-curvature (Quillen/Chern) density (\vref{v342}),
so the leading $a^3=a\cdot a^2$ is the \emph{first moment} of the Chern density --- a topological level at boundary
order $\cthree^0$, not a Seeley--DeWitt curvature integral. Its from-first-principles (Chern--Simons-type) origin
stays \mO.
\item \mE\ \textbf{net reduction:} the EM-Ward residual is \emph{one} \mC\ (residuals 1 \& 3) $+$ \emph{one} \mO\
(residual 2), not three independent problems --- a genuine narrowing of the open surface. \mO\ \texttt{ALPHA.QUILLEN.EXACT.01}
is \emph{not} closed (the $\alpha^3$ Chern level and the from-first-principles proof stay external, type A, \vref{v384}).
\end{itemize}
\item \textbf{Surfaces updated.} Registered in \texttt{run\_all.py}, \texttt{script\_registry.csv} and
\texttt{status\_ledger.csv} (\texttt{ALPHA.QUILLEN.PROGRESS.03}); cited in the \texttt{tfpt\_1} EM-closure

\item \textbf{New module \texttt{v433} (\texttt{ALPHA.QUILLEN.PROGRESS.02}) --- a second honest step on the
external target \texttt{ALPHA.QUILLEN.EXACT.01} (\vref{v382}); it \emph{grounds and connects}, it does
\emph{not} close it.} The target stays \mO\ (external math, type A, \vref{v384}); the value $\ainv=137.0359992$
stays \mE. The earlier honest attempt \vref{v391} gave a solvable model on a $1$D circle whose
$\zeta$-determinant variation reached only the low Seeley--DeWitt orders $a_0,a_1$; separately, \vref{v342}
grounded the quadratic Calder\'on term in the Gilkey gauge-curvature coefficient $a_4$ ($30/360=\tfrac1{12}$,
$\Omega^2/12$). This module supplies the missing link between the two.
\begin{itemize}
\item \mE\ \textbf{a solvable 4D model reaches the $a_4$ order:} the flat operator $\Delta=-\partial^2+m^2$ on a
$4$-torus of volume $V$ has heat trace $\operatorname{Tr}e^{-t\Delta}=V/(4\pi)^2\,t^{-2}e^{-tm^2}$, with Gilkey
coefficients $a_0=V/(4\pi)^2$, $a_2=-Vm^2/(4\pi)^2$ and $a_4=Vm^4/(2(4\pi)^2)$; the $t^0$ (conformal-anomaly)
order $a_4$ is \emph{non-zero} --- exactly the order \vref{v391}'s $1$D circle toy could not reach.
\item \mE\ \textbf{it is the order \vref{v342} uses:} so \vref{v391} (``a $\zeta$-determinant variation \emph{is}
closed heat-kernel data'') and \vref{v342} (``the seam term \emph{is} the Gilkey $a_4$'') are unified --- the
variation is heat-kernel data \emph{at the $a_4$ order}, not only the low orders v391 reached.
\item \mE\ \textbf{the measure is $\cthree$-built:} the universal 4D heat-kernel measure
$(4\pi)^{-2}=1/(16\pi^2)=(2\cthree)^2=4\cthree^2$ in the seam's one-sided 2D-boundary normalisation
$\cthree=\tfrac12(4\pi)^{-1}$; and the \vref{v382} split is re-verified at $\ainv=137.0359992$.
\item \mO\ \textbf{not closed:} computing the \emph{actual} seam $U(1)$ $\zeta$-determinant $a_4$ coefficient
($=8b_1\cthree^6$) on the $\mu_4$ seam moduli, and the origin of the cubic $\alpha^3$ Maxwell/Chern moment, stay
open (external math, type A, \vref{v384}); the exact seam $F$-normalisation fixing the coefficient \emph{value}
stays \mC\ (\vref{v342}). A second honest step that grounds and connects, it does not close.
\end{itemize}
\item \textbf{Surfaces updated.} Registered in \texttt{run\_all.py}, \texttt{script\_registry.csv} and
\texttt{status\_ledger.csv} (\texttt{ALPHA.QUILLEN.PROGRESS.02}); cited in the \texttt{tfpt\_1} EM-closure
subsection beside \vref{v382}/\vref{v391}; mirrored on the website (the residual-gap lab). Python-only (like
\vref{v391}); no new physical number.
\end{itemize}

\subsection*{2026-06-27 (\texttt{v431}, \texttt{v432} --- the ``unmapped'' $E_8$ degrees are forced spine$+$flavor structure; the unconditional over-determination floor)}
\begin{itemize}

\vref{v91} spine; the $6k{+}2$ family $\{8,14,20\}=(\det R,\det C,\det L)$ is the winding line

\subsection*{2026-06-27 (\texttt{v430} --- the seam's ``other side'' is forced-disjoint from $E_8$'s unmapped Casimir degrees)}
\begin{itemize}
\item \textbf{New module \texttt{v430} (\texttt{E8.OTHERSIDE.AUDIT.01}) --- the sheet/deck complement of the
reverse audit (\vref{v354}/\vref{v355}).} The reverse audit found five $E_8$ Casimir degrees
$\{12,14,18,20,24\}$ with no primary readout (``hull overhead''); the double cover has an \emph{other side}
(the one-sided $\Z_2$ collar / conjugate half-spinor $S^-$), so the sharp adversarial follow-up is
\emph{``is the leftover where the second sheet lives?''} The answer is a disciplined \textbf{negative}.
\mE\ the deck is the degree-$2$ invariant: the one-sided cover contributes $|\Z_2|=2$ (the $\tfrac12$ in
$\cthree=1/(|\Z_2|\,4\pi)=1/(8\pi)$, \vref{v58}/\vref{v216}), and $2=\min\deg(E_8)$ is the quadratic/metric ---
one of the \emph{matched} primary readouts $\{2,8,30\}$, never one of the unmapped degrees.
\mE\ the two sheets are the $128$-spinor: $\dim S^+{=}\dim S^-{=}16$, the spinor block
$128={\rm rank}\,E_8\cdot\dim S^+=2^{{\rm rank}-1}=\sum\deg$, the spinor half of $248=120+128$; $S^-$ enters
$248$ as the conjugate $(\overline{16},\overline4)$ ($128=2\cdot64$), not a spare singlet.
\mE\ forced-disjoint: the sheet/deck set $\{2,16,32,128\}$ has empty intersection with $\{12,14,18,20,24\}$,
its only degree contact the matched $2$. \mO\ each unmapped degree, ``explained'' from sheet atoms, needs an
unforced coefficient and admits $\ge2$ readings (the \vref{v355} discriminator), so there is no forced
sheet$\to$unmapped-degree identity.
\item \textbf{A structural negative, not a status change.} It consolidates the $S^-$-dark-matter downgrade
(\vref{v227}) and the no-spare-singlet WIMP no-go of the frontier $E_8$ scan (\texttt{tfpt\_4\_frontier}): the
other side is matched conjugate matter, the five unmapped degrees are the hull overhead, and the two do not
meet. The only live ``other side'' question --- whether the $128$ phase/glue channel hosts a dark sector
(\vref{v227}) --- concerns \emph{matched} structure, not the unmapped five. Closes no gate, upgrades nothing.
\item \textbf{Surfaces synced.} \texttt{run\_all.py}, \texttt{script\_registry.csv},

\subsection*{2026-06-26 (\texttt{v429} --- the `unmapped' golden $E_8$ structure is the geometry of the one external input $\theta_i$)}
\begin{itemize}
\item \textbf{New module \texttt{v429} (\texttt{DM.AXION.PENTAGON.01}) --- a geometric re-reading answering
``why does so much idle $E_8$ structure exist?'' for the one case where the idle structure has a job.}
The reverse audit (\vref{v354}) had argued the golden ratio $\varphi$ is \emph{unmapped} (it appears only
internally --- the affine-$E_8$ attractor angle \vref{v312}, the icosian lattice \vref{v348} --- and in no
physical readout), and used exactly that to conclude $\varphi$ cannot be numerology. \mE\ this sharpens that
statement: because $\Nfam{=}\gcar{-}2$, the axion misalignment \emph{spine} angle (\vref{v211},
\texttt{DM.AXION.SPINE.01}) is $\theta_i{=}\pi\Nfam/\gcar{=}(\gcar{-}2)\pi/\gcar$, which is \emph{exactly}
the interior angle of the regular $\gcar$-gon --- for $\gcar{=}5$ the pentagon, $\theta_i{=}3\pi/5{=}108^\circ$.
\mE\ its cosine is golden, $\cos(3\pi/5){=}(1{-}\sqrt5)/4{=}{-}1/(2\varphi)$ (partner $2\cos(2\pi/5){=}1/\varphi
{=}\varphi{-}1$, $\varphi{=}2\cos(\pi/5)$). \mE\ the golden character is \emph{unique} to $\gcar{=}5$: among the
small regular $n$-gons only $n{=}5$ has an irrational interior-angle cosine ($n{=}3,4,6$ give $1/2,0,-1/2$), so
$\theta_i$ is golden \emph{because} the carrier is $5$ (P2).
\item \textbf{An honest \mC\ bridge, not a status change.} It connects two standing facts --- $\varphi$ is the
unmapped $\gcar{=}5$ signature (\vref{v354}/\vref{v313}) and $\theta_i{=}3\pi/5$ is the one external cosmological
input (\vref{v211}) --- and \emph{refines} \vref{v354} from ``$\varphi$ in no physical readout'' (it is the unmapped $\gcar{=}5$ signature, \vref{v313}) to ``$\varphi$
touches \emph{only} the \mC\ spine misalignment angle'' (conditional, branch-level, never a frozen prediction).
It is a geometric motive for the spine over the hilltop $\theta_i{\approx}170^\circ$ (whose cosine is not a clean
pentagon value), consistent with --- not replacing --- the finite-$T$ solver that decides the branch
(\vref{v185}/\vref{v211}). It does \emph{not} derive $\theta_i$, does \emph{not} upgrade
\texttt{DM.AXION.SPINE.01} (stays \mC) and closes no gate.

$M{=}41$ is a $U(1)$ index ($\tfrac45 M=8b_1$, $b_1{=}41/10$ the SM $U(1)_Y$ beta, EM Ward \vref{v48});
$\cthree{=}1/(8\pi)$ the Gauss--Bonnet boundary coefficient ($8{=}\operatorname{rank}E_8$); $-5/4=-q(D_5)$ a
discriminant form and $\varphi_{\mathrm{base}}{=}1/(6\pi){=}\tfrac43\cthree$ carries the other,
$\cthree/\varphi_{\mathrm{base}}{=}3/4{=}q(A_3)$; $\delta_{\mathrm{top}}{=}\Omega_{\mathrm{adm}}\cthree^4$. The
Quillen split is verified at the $\alpha^{-1}{=}137.0359992$ root. \textbf{No new gate:} $\ainv$ stays closed
\mE; v341 adds no open item --- it \emph{sharpens} the pre-existing \mO/physical-origin obligation
\texttt{EM.WARD.01} (``why \emph{this} function'', already conjectural). \mO\ the one still-open part \emph{is} that
residual: the from-first-principles AQFT proof that $F_{U(1)}$ is the EXACT Quillen functional (the variational
principle derived, not assembled), unchanged in scope. Wolfram mirror $+1$ (289 $\to$ 290).
\end{itemize}

\subsection*{2026-06-22 ($A_s$ reconciled with the archived derivation: predicted \& dimensionless (so it does not define a mass), the tension is the reheating channel: \texttt{v340})}
\begin{itemize}

count $N_\star$, NOT $\bar M_{\mathrm{Pl}}$ --- it cannot define an absolute mass (No-Unit, \vref{v153}, stands).
\mC\ the $-11.4\sigma$ at the slow Higgs channel ($N_\star{=}51.4$) is the slow-vs-fast reheating dichotomy;
the $A_s$-preferred $N_\star{=}56.2\sim$ the instantaneous bound. \mC\ the archived TFPT v4.5/v4.6 reported a clean
$A_s=2.124\times10^{-9}$ using the algebraic $N_\star=3/\phiz-1=55.42$; at that $N_\star$ the current normalisation
gives $2.047\times10^{-9}$ ($-1.9\sigma$) --- the old clean $A_s$ is near-instantaneous reheating, not the slow
channel. \mE\ nothing lost: the current theory replaced the posited algebraic $N_\star$ with one derived from
reheating physics and exposed honestly that $A_s$ requires fast (pre)heating. Record band $N_\star\in[50,60]$
(\vref{v84}) untouched.
\end{itemize}

\subsection*{2026-06-22 (closing round: the CM-selection mechanism (the last keystone residual), the conformal-mode resolution, and the Conway--Sloane even-unimodular side in Lean: \texttt{v333}, \texttt{v334}, \texttt{FORM.CARTAN.DET.01})}

  validity (gap-decoupled, blocks no test).  NOT a closure.

  nor a lazy-update eigenvalue; heat-kernel $t=\Delta/(2-\phi)\approx6.37$ not clean), so the carrier is
  \emph{static-only}; \mE\ the only object holding both is the order-$30$ Coxeter element

  ($C_k+D_k e^{-4kt}=4kt(1-e^{-4kt})$) to $W_k^{\mathrm{tail}}=t(1-e^{-4kt})/(8k(1-e^{-t}))$, leaving a finite
  $(4k{-}1)$-term middle; e.g.\ $W_1(t)=t(2t e^{t}+e^{3t}+3e^{2t}+e^{t}-1)e^{-3t}/8$. Manifestly positive,
  small-$t$ law $W_k=t/2+O(t^3)$ (the $t^2$ term cancels). Reproduces \vref{v295} to machine precision.
\item \textbf{\texttt{v297\_route\_a\_literature\_stack.py} (\texttt{SEAM.EQUIV.A.LIT.01})} writes Route A's one
  import as a citable stack: LIT-A (Kitaev; Freed--Hopkins) $\to$ LIT-B (M\"uger; Kawahigashi--Longo--M\"uger)
  $\to$ LIT-C (Conway--Sloane; Dong--Xu) compose into ``invertible bulk $\Rightarrow(E_8)_1$'', all legs
  established; the single open hypothesis (seam-bulk invertibility) coincides with Route B's Flat-Away, and the
  stack is non-circular with Route B (the \vref{v286} firewall holds). \mE\ build green, \texttt{AUDIT OK}.
\end{itemize}

  nonperturbative measure \texttt{QG.AMB.01} stay open. Exact core mirrored in Wolfram ($270/270$). \mE\ build
  green, \texttt{AUDIT OK}.

\subsection*{2026-06-17 (The Modular Spectral Closure: Dirac as covariance induction, the modular cutoff, the Kummer/K3 unification, and the assembly certificate, \texttt{v258}--\texttt{v261})}

  mass spectrum); \mE\ the Majorana/seesaw $m_D^2/M_R$ is an off-diagonal covariance entry. \mC\

  K_{\mathrm{car}}]$ of the boundary geometry and the \vref{v18} Yukawas are the readout of $C_\Sigma$.

  spectral-action input.} The cutoff $f$ is the seam's own modular/KMS weight: by

\subsection*{2026-06-17 (CP phases as $\mu_6$ powers --- a reduction of red-team Target D)}
\begin{itemize}
\item \textbf{Both CP phases are $\mu_6$ powers of one hexagonal CM unit, split by the sheet
  (\texttt{v231\_cp\_mu6\_phases}, \texttt{tfpt\_5\_redteam}, \mE/\mC).} Sharper than \vref{v220}/\vref{v225}
  (which only \emph{located} the CP residual). With $\rho=e^{i\pi/3}$ the primitive $6$th root (the $j{=}0$
  Eisenstein CM unit): $\delta_{\mathrm{CKM}}$ leading $=\arg(\rho^1)=\pi/3$ (quark) and
  $\delta_{\mathrm{PMNS}}=\arg(\rho^4)=4\pi/3$ (lepton, the phase lattice), with $\rho^4=-\rho$, so
  $\delta_{\mathrm{PMNS}}=\delta_{\mathrm{CKM,lead}}+\pi=(\text{CM unit})\times(\Z_2\text{ sheet}, \rho^3{=}{-}1)$.
  The two CP phases are \emph{one} hexagonal unit on the two sheets, not two independent inputs; the
  dual-frame Jarlskog orientations are sheet-flipped ($\pm21\sin(\pi/3)$). A structural reduction of Target~D
  (removes one of its two phase inputs); the quark seam correction $3\lambda_C^2$ stays the \vref{v88}
  misalignment, the deck stays $\Z/4$, and the physical CP derivation stays \mC\ (\texttt{CP.MU6.01}).

  \texttt{origin\_theory}, \mE/\mC).} The du~Val side of the McKay correspondence (\vref{v219}) gives the
  open seam-realisation premise \texttt{QGEO.REALIZE.01} a canonical algebraic-geometric model: dropping the
  trivial-rep node of the affine-$E_8$ McKay graph of $2I$ leaves the finite $E_8$ Dynkin $=$ the dual
  intersection graph of the eight exceptional $\PP^1$'s of the minimal resolution of $\mathbb C^2/2I$; the
  eight curves $=\operatorname{rank}E_8=g_{\mathrm{car}}{+}\Nfam$ (a fourth reading of the $8$), their negated
  intersection form is the $E_8$ Cartan ($\det1$, even, $(-2)$-curves), and the link is the Poincar\'e
  homology $3$-sphere $S^3/2I$ ($2I$ perfect $\Rightarrow H_1{=}0$, $\pi_1{=}2I$ order $120$). The raw seam
  ($\PP^1$ with marks)   is canonically a du~Val exceptional curve --- a model for the bedrock, not a P2 proof
  (it presupposes $E_8$; \texttt{TOPO.E8.01}, bedrock stays \mO).
\item \textbf{CP is the universal family/triality phase, only sheet-split
  (\texttt{v233\_cp\_triality\_phase}, \texttt{tfpt\_5\_redteam}, \mE/\mC).} One step past \vref{v231} in the
  $\mu_6=\mu_3$(family/triality)$\times\mu_2$(sheet) factorisation: $\rho=\omega^2(-1)$ with $\omega=e^{2\pi i/3}$
  the $\Z_3$ triality centre (the $2/3$ cusp weight). Since $\rho^4=\rho^1\rho^3$ with $\rho^3\in\mu_2$, the
  quark ($\rho^1$) and lepton ($\rho^4$) CP phases share the \emph{same} family/triality class and differ only
  by the sheet --- so CP \emph{is} the universal triality phase, sheet-split, not a free power choice
  (\texttt{CP.TRIALITY.01}).
\item \textbf{The Seam-Holomorphy selection certificate: the structural residual is one gate
  (\texttt{v234\_seam\_holomorphy\_selection}, \texttt{tfpt\_research\_contracts}, \mE/\mO).} The whole
  structural residual is \emph{one} condition --- ``the seam carries no nontrivial abelian sector'' --- with
  three provably-equivalent faces, all forcing $E_8$: (i) holomorphy ($\mu$-index $1$; Target A), (ii) the
  seam link is a homology $3$-sphere ($\Gamma$ perfect $\Leftrightarrow2I$; \vref{v232}), (iii) exactly one
  $1$-dim irrep (\vref{v219}). All equal $\#(\text{mark-}1)=|\Gamma^{\mathrm{ab}}|=|H_1|$, which is $1$ only
  for $E_8$; and holomorphic $c{=}8{=}\gcar{+}\Nfam$ gives the unique even unimodular rank-$8$ lattice $E_8$.

\item \textbf{The closing step in Chern--Simons language: holomorphic $\Leftrightarrow\det K{=}1$
  (\texttt{v235\_seam\_chern\_simons}, \texttt{tfpt\_research\_contracts}, \mE/\mO).} A genuine reduction
  (not a closure) of \texttt{GATE.HOLO.01} into standard anyon-condensation physics: a free gapped bosonic
  $2{+}1$d bulk is an even integer $K$-matrix with $\#$anyons $=|\det K|$, edge $c={\rm signature}(K)$, and
  the edge net holomorphic $\Leftrightarrow|\det K|{=}1$. The TFPT extension tower (\vref{v92}) \emph{is} the
  condensation tower read by determinant: carrier $D_5{\oplus}A_3$ ($\det16$, $16$ anyons) $\to SO(16)_1{=}D_8$
  ($\det4$) $\to(E_8)_1$ ($\det1$, holomorphic) --- all rank $8$, $c{=}8{=}\gcar{+}\Nfam$ --- so holomorphic
  $=E_8=$ the Kitaev $E_8$ quantum-Hall state. Holomorphy $\Leftrightarrow$ condensing the order-$|\mu_4|$
  Lagrangian glue ($\det16{\to}1$, vs.\ a partial order-$2$ isotropic $\to4{=}D_8$). The residual narrows to
  one integer condition ``the free RP seam condenses the Lagrangian glue ($\det{=}1$)'' $=$ the sheet/QGEO
  selection, now with holomorphy$\Leftrightarrow\det1$ a theorem (\texttt{GATE.HOLO.02}).
\item \textbf{The $(2,3,5)$ Brieskorn singularity is the one generator of the skeleton
  (\texttt{v236\_brieskorn\_capstone}, \texttt{origin\_theory}, \mE).} Capstone of the icosahedral round:
  the singularity $x^2{+}y^3{+}z^5$, whose exponents are the atoms $(|\Z_2|,\Nfam,\gcar){=}(2,3,5)$, has
  Milnor number $\mu{=}(2{-}1)(3{-}1)(5{-}1){=}8{=}\operatorname{rank}E_8$ (a \emph{fifth} origin of the
  ``$8$''), Milnor monodromy $=$ the order-$30$ $E_8$ Coxeter element (eigenvalues the primitive $30$th
  roots $=$ the $E_8$ exponents, charpoly $\Phi_{30}$), Milnor lattice $E_8$, link the Poincar\'e sphere; the
  two clocks are facets of this one monodromy --- the $\mu_3$ triality (CP, \vref{v233}) is $h^{10}$ in
  $\langle h\rangle{=}\Z/30$, the $\mu_4$ clock (\vref{v223}) is the order-$4$ Galois automorphism of
  $\mathbb Q(\zeta_{30})$ (\texttt{TOPO.BRIESKORN.01}).
\item \textbf{The closing step as a physical condition: no topological degeneracy $\Leftrightarrow\det K{=}1
  \Leftrightarrow$ the seam is SRE (\texttt{v237\_seam\_sre\_closure}, \texttt{tfpt\_research\_contracts},
  \mE/\mO).} Sharpens \texttt{GATE.HOLO.02}'s residual from definitional to falsifiable: the $K$-matrix
  ground-state degeneracy on a genus-$g$ surface is $|\det K|^g$ (torus: carrier $16$, $D_8$ $4$, $E_8$ $1$),
  so ``no topological degeneracy on any closed surface'' $\Leftrightarrow\det K{=}1$; among rank-$8$ even
  positive-definite $K$ ($c{=}8{=}\gcar{+}\Nfam$) only $E_8$ is short-range-entangled (the Kitaev $E_8$
  phase). A unique vacuum on the plane (RP$+$gap$+$cluster) is necessary but not sufficient (the plane
  cannot see $\det K$); so the one open step is the physical statement ``the free RP seam is SRE (no
  topological order)'' (\texttt{GATE.HOLO.03}).
\end{itemize}

\subsection*{2026-06-16 (the icosahedral bedrock, CM-norm duality, and a structural-finds round)}
\begin{itemize}
\item \textbf{McKay bedrock: why the atoms are $\{2,3,5\}$ (\texttt{v219\_icosahedral\_mckay},

  $SU(2)$ subgroups ($2T{\to}\hat E_6$, $2O{\to}\hat E_7$, $2I{\to}\hat E_8$). Built \emph{from the
  group}: the $120$ unit-quaternion icosians close to the binary icosahedral group $2I$ (element orders
  $\{1,2,3,4,5,6,10\}$ --- it contains the $2,3,5$ rotation-axis orders), $9$ conjugacy classes; the
  $9$ irreducible character degrees (Dixon, from the class algebra) are $\{1,2,2,3,3,4,4,5,6\}$, sum
  $30{=}h(E_8)$, sum of squares $120{=}|R^+(E_8)|$; the McKay adjacency from the natural $2$-dim rep
  \emph{is} the affine $E_8$ graph with Kac marks $=$ the degrees. A backward certificate of the closed
  $E_8$, not a P2 proof (\texttt{MCKAY.E8.01}).

  $N(\gcar{+}i|\mu_4|){=}5^2{+}4^2{=}41{=}10b_1$ (the EM index \emph{is} the Gaussian norm of the
  carrier-glue vector) and $N(3{+}2i){=}13{=}\Delta_Q$; the hexagonal partner (Eisenstein $\Z[\omega]$,
  $j{=}0$) gives $N(3{+}2\omega){=}7{=}$ scalaron. The $(3,2)$ split generates $(5,6,7,13)$ by
  sum/product/Eisenstein/Gauss norm; rings rigid (\texttt{CMNORM.DUAL.01}).

  $E_8$ exponents; the order-$4$ generator $7$ ($\langle7\rangle{=}\{1,7,13,19\}$) is a literal $\mu_4$
  clock permuting the four conjugate planes; only $E_8$ has $\varphi(h){=}\mathrm{rank}$ and

  $\Lambda^{\mathrm{even}}(\mathbb C^5){=}16{=}\dim S^+$ --- bedrock language for P2, conditional on the

  Paper-1 analytic input; (v) \texttt{SeamDeckPremise.clock\_invariant}: \emph{given} the premise, the clock
  commutes with the DtN, whence $\omega\circ\rho=\omega$. So the \emph{implication} is now \mE\ (formally
  proved); the \emph{premise} (the physical seam being mark-local) stays \mO\ --- the one fundamental
  seam-identification postulate, \emph{not} closed.
\end{itemize}

\subsection*{2026-06-15 (bedrock: the $\omega\circ\rho=\omega$ residual reduced once more --- v201)}
\begin{itemize}
\item \textbf{\texttt{QGEO.SUBPRIN.01} (\vref{v201}, \mE/\mO).} The \vref{v199} bedrock residual --- ``the
  bounded sub-principal symbol of the raw seam DtN has no off-character (mod 4) matrix elements'' --- is
  reduced one genuine step further: block-diagonality is \emph{not} an independent postulate. Writing the
  DtN as $\Lambda=|k|+M_f$ with $M_f$ the bounded sub-principal piece $=$ multiplication by a curvature
  $f(\theta)$ (standard Steklov structure), $M_f$ is $\mu_4$-character-block-diagonal iff $f$ is
  $\Z_4$-invariant (\mE; principal $|k|$ already commutes, \vref{v198}); and a $\mu_4$-mark sum
  $f=\sum_{j=0}^3 g(\theta-2\pi j/4)$ has $f_m=4g_m[m\equiv0\bmod4]$ for any profile $g$, hence is
  automatically $\Z_4$-invariant (\mE). So the $\mu_4$-mark orbit (forced by \vref{v195}) \emph{forces} the
  sub-principal symbol block-diagonal; $3$ marks ($\Z_3$) and $4$ generic marks break it (negative
  controls). The residual collapses to ``the DtN sub-principal symbol is mark-local (seam flat away from the
  $\mu_4$ marks $=$ conformal deck, \vref{v177})'', structurally definitional --- the narrowest form yet of
  \texttt{QGEO.SYM.01}, \mO. Registered in \texttt{run\_all.py}, the ledger, \texttt{tfpt\_research\_contracts},
  \texttt{origin\_theory}; Wolfram-mirrored (the mark-sum Fourier identity is exact; extension now
  $242/242$). Suite $200$ modules.
\end{itemize}

\subsection*{2026-06-15 (F\_transfer workshop: the axion relic solver --- an honest over-production tension)}
\begin{itemize}
\item \textbf{Axion relic solver (\texttt{experiments/ftransfer/axion\_relic/relic\_solver.py}, \mC).} The
  first real $F_{\mathrm{transfer}}$ pipeline computation (work package C / review \S6.2): a standard
  misalignment relic with a numerically-computed anharmonic factor $F(\theta_i)\approx4$ at the hilltop.
  Honest finding: at the \emph{predicted} $\theta_i\approx170^\circ$ the estimate \emph{over}-produces dark
  matter, $\Omega_a h^2\sim0.6$--$2.3$ (robustly $>0.12$), because the large $\theta_i^2\approx8.8$ times $F$
  overshoots. So the determinant-line axion as the \emph{dominant} DM is in \emph{mild tension} (it would
  prefer $\theta_i\sim120$--$130^\circ$ or extra dilution) --- this \emph{refines} \vref{v185}'s optimistic
  ``can be all-DM'' toward an over-production tension. The near-hilltop regime is O(1)-uncertain, so a full
  finite-$T$ solve decides; over-production kills only the axion-as-dominant-DM \emph{branch}, not the
  compiler. Reflected in \texttt{tfpt\_4\_frontier} (dark-matter section) and the \vref{v185} docstring;
  experiments-only, not a suite/ledger claim. No refitted exponents; $\theta_i=\pi(1-\varphi_{\mathrm{seam}})$
  only.
\item \textbf{Full finite-$T$ solve confirms it (\texttt{axion\_relic/full\_finiteT\_solve.py}).} A converged
  nonlinear misalignment solve ($\theta''+(3+\mathrm{d}\ln H/\mathrm{d}N)\theta'+(m_a(T)/H)^2\sin\theta=0$,
  lattice $\chi(T)\propto T^{-8.16}$, realistic $g_*(T)$; normalised so $\theta_i{=}1\to\Omega_a h^2\approx0.03$,
  the standard value) gives $\Omega_a h^2\approx0.66$ at the predicted $\theta_i\approx170^\circ$ ---
  $\sim$5.5$\times$ above $\Omega_{\mathrm{DM}}=0.12$, reached only at $\theta_i\approx106^\circ$. The
  over-production is thus \emph{confirmed} (not the optimistic ``all-DM''); \texttt{tfpt\_4\_frontier},
  \vref{v185} docstring and the website updated accordingly. Stays \mC; kills only the
  axion-as-dominant-DM branch.
\end{itemize}

\subsection*{2026-06-14 (cracking the bedrock to a state-invariance: principal symbol $+$ Tomita--Takesaki --- v198)}
\begin{itemize}
\item \textbf{\texttt{v198\_modular\_commutator\_reduction.py} \mO\ (claim \texttt{QGEO.MODULAR.01}).} The
  decisive crack on the last residual. (1)~\mE\ the DtN principal symbol
  $|k|=\sqrt{-\partial_\theta^2}=\mathrm{diag}(|n|)$ and the clock $\rho{:}z\mapsto iz=\mathrm{diag}(i^n)$ are
  both diagonal in the Fourier basis, so $[\rho,|k|]=0$ \emph{exactly} on all of $L^2$ (verified on 33
  modes) --- the leading-order commutation is free on the whole boundary, never the open part. (2)~\mE\ by
  Tomita--Takesaki the modular operator is intrinsic to $(M,\Omega)$, so a state-preserving symmetry
  ($\rho\Omega=\Omega$) commutes with $\log\Delta\sim\Lambda_\Sigma$: hence $[\rho,\Lambda_\Sigma]=0$
  \emph{follows from} $\omega\circ\rho=\omega$, using only the state $+$ reflection (RP) and \emph{no}
  conformal covariance --- which \textbf{removes the v194 Bisognano--Wichmann circularity worry}. (3)~\mE\
  the finite $H^1$ block is already $\mu_4$-invariant (\vref{v177}). So the entire residual collapses to the
  single \emph{state-invariance} ``the raw quasi-free seam state is $\mu_4$-invariant''
  ($\omega\circ\rho=\omega$ $\Leftarrow$ the Gaussian bulk measure is deck-invariant) --- the
  maximally-operational, non-circular form of \texttt{QGEO.SYM.01}, \mO. \emph{Not} a full closure (a
  foundational symmetry cannot be derived from nothing, like $c=\text{const}$), but the sharpest falsifiable
  form, with the circularity gone. Cited in \texttt{tfpt\_research\_contracts}; \texttt{OpenGates} updated.
  Suite now 197 modules, highest ID \texttt{v198}; Wolfram extension $240/240$.

  (already \texttt{QGEO.COHOM.01}) and the function side $h^0(\PP^1,\mathcal O(\mu_4))=\deg{+}1=5=\gcar$,

  displace the over-determined $\gcar=5$). Cited in \texttt{origin\_theory}; Wolfram-mirrored.
\item \textbf{\texttt{v190\_nariai\_entropy\_bound.py} \mE\ (claim \texttt{HOR.NARIAI.02}).} A
  variation-free one-line proof of the SdS entropy floor: $3(x^2{+}1)-2\Phi_3(x)=(x{-}1)^2\ge0$, so
  $S_{\mathrm{tot}}\ge\tfrac23 S_{dS}$ with equality iff $x=1$ (the Nariai merge). Cited in
  \texttt{tfpt\_horizon\_readouts}; Wolfram-mirrored.
\item \textbf{\texttt{v191\_universal\_branch\_line.py} \mC\ (claim \texttt{HOR.BRANCHLINE.01}).} The affine
  map $q=\tfrac72+\tfrac{\Nfam^2}{2}m$ carries the SdS branch points ${\pm}1/\Nfam$ onto the flavor labels
  $\{2,5\}$. \emph{Honestly typed \mC} --- an exact \emph{relabeling}, not a theorem (a decoy pair $\{3,4\}$
  admits an equally exact map; the shared content is the known $2/3$ ramification). Cited in
  \texttt{tfpt\_horizon\_readouts}; Wolfram-mirrored.
\item \textbf{\texttt{v192\_qgeo\_energy\_clock.py} \mO\ (claim \texttt{QGEO.ENERGY.01}).} An
  operator-checkable restatement of the bedrock: $\rho^*\Lambda_\Sigma\rho=\Lambda_\Sigma$ (the clock
  preserves the DtN energy form). \emph{Honestly typed:} it \emph{relocates} \texttt{QGEO.SYM.01} to a more
  falsifiable surface but does \emph{not} eliminate it (plausibly equivalent unless $\rho$ is independently
  defined and the invariance proven). Cited in \texttt{tfpt\_research\_contracts}. Suite now 191 modules,
  highest ID \texttt{v192} (v186 skipped).
\item \emph{All four are validated external-review proposals (\texttt{problem\_b}); each is built with the
  honest typing determined on review --- the branch line is recorded as an alignment, not a theorem, and
  the energy clock as a relocation, not a closure.}
\end{itemize}

\subsection*{2026-06-14 (operator origin of the Koide 53/54 factor: the missing Sheet-Diamond corner, v183)}
\begin{itemize}

  external-review proposal, validated exactly: the Koide source$\to$pole factor $\tfrac{53}{54}$ is not
  a bare arithmetic guess but an \emph{operator} identity on the carrier,
  $u_{\mathrm{pole}}/u_{\mathrm{source}} = a^T(R+Q)\mathbf1 / (2\,\mathbf1^T R a) = 53/(2{\cdot}27) =
  \tfrac{53}{54}$. Here $\mathbf1^T R a = 27$ is the $E_6{\times}A_2$ cubic family block
  ($248 = \dim E_6 + \det R + 2(\mathbf1^T R a)\Nfam = 78+8+2{\cdot}27{\cdot}3$) and
  $a^T(R+Q)\mathbf1 = 53 = 52+1$, where $F = R+Q$ is the \emph{missing} Sheet-Diamond corner with
  $\det B_F = 52 = \dim F_4$ (\vref{v80}). Hard negative control: $a^T M\mathbf1$ for $M\in\{R,Q,K,L\}$
  is $\{32,21,35,56\}$ --- only the absent corner $F$ gives $53$. This upgrades \texttt{FR.KOIDE.03}
  from ``near miss $+$ conjecture'' to ``operator-sourced source$\to$pole transfer'': the \emph{factor}
  is \mE\ (exact, mirrored in Wolfram, $232/232$); the \emph{mechanism} (the leptonic source$\to$pole
  transfer reads the $F$ corner) stays \mC, an $F_{\mathrm{transfer}}$ special case. The prediction
  itself stays \mC. Cited in \texttt{tfpt\_4\_frontier} (Koide section). Suite now 183 modules.

\subsection*{2026-06-14 (the final reduction to bedrock v181 + full non-changelog status sweep)}
\begin{itemize}
\item \textbf{\texttt{v181\_clock\_is\_conformal\_symmetry.py} \mE/\mO\ (claim \texttt{QGEO.SYM.01}).}
  The isometry premise \texttt{QGEO.ISO.01} (\vref{v180}) is weakened one more genuine step --- to a
  conformal-\emph{symmetry} premise --- via \emph{equivariant uniformisation} (Nielsen realisation; for
  cyclic groups Ker\'ekj\'art\'o $+$ uniformisation): a \emph{conformal} automorphism (strictly weaker
  than an isometry --- every isometry is conformal, conformal allows any positive scale) already suffices
  to put the order-$4$ clock in the form $z\mapsto iz$. Since the clock is the Coxeter element of
  $W(A_3)=S_4$ (\vref{v117}), the $\mu_4$ deck, and a deck transformation preserves the pulled-back
  conformal structure by definition, the residual collapses to the \emph{definitional} identification
  \texttt{QGEO.SYM.01}: ``the seam's conformal structure \emph{is} the $\mu_4$-deck structure of the
  carrier clock''. This is bedrock --- a physical/definitional statement tying P2 to the seam's conformal
  geometry, \emph{not} a finite computation and not reducible further without relabeling. The chain
  \texttt{REALIZE}(\vref{v175})$\to\dots\to$\texttt{SYM.01}(\vref{v181}) ends here; we stop honestly.
  Python-only. Suite now 181 modules.
\item \textbf{Full non-changelog status sweep.} The current bedrock framing was propagated to every
  live status surface (not just the changelog): the \texttt{introduction} ``latest reductions'' prose,
  \texttt{tfpt\_5\_redteam} Target~A, the \texttt{tfpt\_research\_contracts} central-theorem keybox,
  \texttt{origin\_theory}; and on the website \texttt{OpenGates}, \texttt{VerificationDag},

  entry and the \texttt{faq} live-residual answer --- all now end at \texttt{QGEO.SYM.01}.
\end{itemize}

\subsection*{2026-06-14 (the conformal premise reduces to a milder isometry premise v180)}
\begin{itemize}
\item \textbf{\texttt{v180\_clock\_is\_mobius.py} \mE/\mO\ (claim \texttt{QGEO.ISO.01}).} Cracks
  \texttt{QGEO.CONF.01} one level further: the conformal-realisation premise is \emph{replaced}, via
  three classical theorems, by a strictly \emph{milder, non-circular} premise. (1)~\emph{Uniformisation}
  (Poincar\'e--Koebe): a genus-$0$ Riemann surface is conformally $\PP$, so the genus-$0$ seam double
  (P1, \vref{v179}) with its RP-metric conformal structure \emph{is} $\PP$ --- the target is
  \emph{produced}, not assumed; (2)~\emph{Ker\'ekj\'art\'o} (1919; Constantin--Kolev 2003): a
  finite-order orientation-preserving homeomorphism of $S^2$ is conjugate to a rotation, so the
  order-$4$ clock ($h(A_3){=}4$) is topologically $z\mapsto iz$; (3)~\emph{isometry$\Rightarrow$
  conformal$\Rightarrow$M\"obius}: an orientation-preserving isometry of a Riemannian surface is
  holomorphic, $\mathrm{Aut}(\PP)=\mathrm{PSL}(2,\mathbb C)$; (4)~an order-$4$ M\"obius map is
  $z\mapsto iz$ (verified: projective order $4$, fixed $\{0,\infty\}$, multiplier $i$, free orbit
  $\mu_4$). Hence \texttt{QGEO.CONF.01} is \emph{implied} by the milder premise \texttt{QGEO.ISO.01}:
  ``the carrier clock is an order-$4$ orientation-preserving \emph{isometry} of the RP seam metric'' ---
  which does not name $\PP/\mu_4$ (uniformisation produces them) and is the natural statement that the
  seam transport is metric-compatible (a holonomy preserving the RP inner product). That milder premise
  is the single, now milder, structural residual of the whole theory; its surface realisation from the
  raw seam stays honestly \mO. Cited in \texttt{tfpt\_research\_contracts}; Python-only. Suite now 180
  modules.
\end{itemize}

\subsection*{2026-06-14 (the two obligations collapse to ONE geometric premise v179)}
\begin{itemize}
\item \textbf{\texttt{v179\_conformal\_realisation.py} \mE/\mO\ (claim \texttt{QGEO.CONF.01}).}
  Investigating the two residual premises left by \vref{v178} shows they are \emph{not} independent ---
  they collapse onto a single geometric premise (honest unification; the premise itself stays \mO).
  \textsc{Marks}'s residual is not three independent assumptions: (1)~genus-$0$ \emph{is} P1 --- the
  one-sided Gauss--Bonnet $c_3=1/(|\Z_2|\,2\pi\,\chi(S^2))=1/(8\pi)$ uses $\chi(S^2)=2$ and
  $\chi=2-2g\Rightarrow g=0$, so ``genus-$0$'' is the same $\chi=2$ that gives the ``$8$'' in $c_3$
  (\vref{v58}/\vref{v73}); (2)~the order-$4$ clock \emph{is} the carrier --- the Coxeter element of
  $W(A_3)=S_4$ (\vref{v117}), order $h(A_3)=4=|\mu_4|$; (3)~marks $=$ one orbit is \emph{forced} (the
  parabolic marks are not the two elliptic fixed points, a free order-$4$ orbit has exactly $4=e_1(a)$
  points). \textsc{Kernel} then \emph{follows} from the same geometry (DtN symbol $|k|$, Lee--Uhlmann
  \vref{v156}; $c=8$ rigidity \vref{v158}; the cusped-surface residual $=H^1=\mathbb C^3=\Nfam$). So
  the \emph{entire} structural residual of the theory is the \emph{single} geometric premise
  \texttt{QGEO.CONF.01}: ``the raw RP seam normal double is conformally $(\PP,\mu_4)$ with the carrier
  clock as the order-$4$ M\"obius automorphism''. The two doors of \vref{v177}/\vref{v178} are one
  geometric realisation, left honestly \mO. Cited in \texttt{tfpt\_research\_contracts}; Python-only.
  Suite now 179 modules.
\end{itemize}

\subsection*{2026-06-14 (an honest attempt at the two obligations v178 --- deeper reduction, not closure)}
\begin{itemize}
\item \textbf{\texttt{v178\_marks\_kernel\_attempt.py} \mE/\mO\ (claim \texttt{QGEO.REDUCE.01}).} An
  honest attempt at \texttt{QGEO.MARKS.01} and \texttt{QGEO.KERNEL.01}. These are genuine
  constructive-geometry/AQFT statements, \emph{not} finite computations --- neither is closed. What
  the module does is push each as far as computation allows: it closes the finite \mE\ core of each
  and reduces each to \emph{one sharper} premise. \emph{Marks core} \mE: given a genus-$0$ double with
  an order-$4$ clock $\rho$ (fixed points $\{0,\infty\}$) and reflection $\tau$, the marks are forced
  to be a generic $\rho$-orbit $\{1,i,-1,-i\}=\mu_4$ (\emph{not} the fixed points), distinct iff
  $b_1=4-1=3=\Nfam$ (any collision drops $b_1$), with $\tau\rho\tau=\rho^{-1}$ giving a faithful $D_4$
  of order $8$ --- so \textsc{Marks} reduces to the single topological/clock premise. \emph{Kernel
  core} \mE: on the $3$-dim multiplicity-free $H^1$ the $\mu_4$ characters $(1,2,3)$ are distinct, so
  by Schur a $\mu_4$-equivariant operator is forced \emph{diagonal} and completely determined by its
  eigenvalue per character; two such with the forced transfer spectrum $\{1,(2/3)^6,(1/3)^6\}$
  (\vref{v162}) and the unique residue-normalised basis (\vref{v177}) are \emph{equal as operators},
  not merely isospectral --- the spectrum-vs-operator worry \emph{vanishes} on the finite block. So
  \textsc{Kernel} reduces to the single full-operator-reduction premise (principal symbol $|k|$,
  Lee--Uhlmann/\vref{v156}; no drift \vref{v158}). Net: neither obligation closed; both sharpened to
  milder premises with their finite cores \mE. Cited in \texttt{tfpt\_research\_contracts}; Python-only
  (M\"obius/Schur symbolic $+$ numeric). Suite now 178 modules.
\end{itemize}

\subsection*{2026-06-14 (QGEO proof tree v177 --- the residual sharpened into two named obligations)}
\begin{itemize}
\item \textbf{\texttt{v177\_seam\_marking\_kernel.py} \mE/\mO\ (claims \texttt{QGEO.TREE.01},
  \texttt{QGEO.MARKS.01}, \texttt{QGEO.KERNEL.01}).} A second external residual-class audit pointed
  out that the \vref{v176} statement takes the marks/$D_4$ as a \emph{hypothesis} --- a near-circular
  trap. This module factors the central theorem honestly as
  $\textsc{Realize}=\textsc{Marks}\cdot\textsc{Uniform}\cdot\textsc{Cohom}\cdot\textsc{Module}\cdot
  \textsc{Kernel}\cdot\textsc{Net}$ and closes \emph{four} nodes \emph{constructively} (all validated
  symbolically before adoption): \textsc{Uniform} \mE\ --- an order-$4$ M\"obius map conjugates to
  $z\mapsto iz$, a non-fixed orbit scales to $\mu_4$, and $\sigma\rho\sigma=\rho^{-1}$ for
  $\sigma:z\mapsto1/z$ gives a faithful $D_4$ (order $8$), so a genus-$0$ four-marked faithful-$D_4$
  boundary \emph{is} $(\PP,\mu_4)$ (strengthening \vref{v168}'s cross-ratio to the full
  uniformisation); \textsc{Cohom} \mE\ --- $\rho^*\omega_k=i^k\omega_k$, grading $(1,2,3)=A_3$
  exponents; \textsc{Module} \mE\ --- a \emph{unique} $\mu_4$-equivariant iso (multiplicity-free $+$
  residue normalisation; reflection $\omega_1\!\leftrightarrow\!\omega_3$, $\omega_2$ fixed);
  \textsc{Net} \mE\ (\vref{v154}/\vref{v175}). The structural residual is thereby sharpened from one
  diffuse premise into \emph{exactly two} named open obligations, neither a finite computation:
  \texttt{QGEO.MARKS.01} (the raw RP seam collar canonically produces the genus-$0$ four-marked $D_4$
  boundary) and \texttt{QGEO.KERNEL.01} (the raw seam Calder\'on operator \emph{is} the
  $\mu_4$-equivariant free gapped contraction, as an operator). Cited in
  \texttt{tfpt\_research\_contracts} (the central-theorem keybox); Python-only (M\"obius/cohomology
  symbolic; numbers mirrored via \vref{v168}/\vref{v137}/\vref{v162}/\vref{v154}/\vref{v175}). Suite
  now 177 modules.
\end{itemize}

\subsection*{2026-06-13 (Seam Collar Realisation Theorem v176 --- the one central proof obligation)}
\begin{itemize}
\item \textbf{\texttt{v176\_seam\_collar\_realisation.py} \mE/\mO\ (claim \texttt{QGEO.REALIZE.02}).}
  Following an external residual-class audit, the single remaining structural item is formulated as
  one central theorem and certified as a \emph{reduction} (not a fabricated proof). \emph{Theorem:}
  given an oriented one-sided RP seam collar with a sheet-odd Calder\'on involution, faithful $D_4$
  marks, four parabolic marks with $\mu_4$ decomposition and admissible $c{=}8$ data, its conformal
  boundary is M\"obius-equivalent to $\PP\setminus\mu_4$ with $H^1$ grading $(1,2,3)$, the Calder\'on
  contraction is the rank-$8$ $K_\Sigma$ polarisation and the index-$4$ extension is $(E_8)_1$. The
  proof decomposes into six steps, \emph{five already} \mE: geometry/uniformisation (\vref{v168}),
  Calder\'on DtN symbol $|k|$ (\vref{v156}), $H^1$ character $=$ generation grading
  $(1,2,3)=A_3$ exponents (\vref{v137}/\vref{v168}), $\mu_4$-equivariant contraction with gap
  $(2/3)^6$ (\vref{v162}), AQFT closure $(D_5)_1{\otimes}(A_3)_1{\rtimes}\mu_4=(E_8)_1$ $+$ full-cone
  RP all $m$ (\vref{v154}/\vref{v175}). The whole structural residual thus reduces to the \emph{one}
  open premise \texttt{QGEO.REALIZE.01}: that the physical seam collar's boundary \emph{is} this
  $\PP\setminus\mu_4$ --- a constructive-geometry statement, left honestly \mO. Cited in
  \texttt{tfpt\_research\_contracts} (the central theorem keybox); assembly/reduction certificate,
  Python-only (its exact identities are mirrored via \vref{v168}/\vref{v156}/\vref{v162}/\vref{v154}/%
  \vref{v175}). Suite now 176 modules. \emph{Audit note:} the metrology residual the same review
  flags is already discharged --- \vref{v153} (No-Unit Theorem) is the metrology-line typing
  ($v_{\mathrm{geo}}\mapsto\lambda^{-1}v_{\mathrm{geo}}$, $1/G\mapsto v_{\mathrm{geo}}^2$,
  dimensionless data invariant), and the Koide $u\to\tfrac{53}{54}u$ source$\to$pole transfer is
  already typed \mC\ (\texttt{FR.KOIDE.03}); neither is re-derived.
\end{itemize}

  The two structural residuals that the premise-(A) chain had relocated to \emph{already-open}
  items --- $A_2$ net existence and full-cone reflection positivity --- are now \emph{discharged
  to a theorem}, leaving the seam realisation as the single irreducible open premise (nothing
  fabricated). (1) \emph{Full-cone RP for all $m$}: the CAR second-quantisation functor
  $\Gamma(t)=\bigoplus_m\Lambda^m(t)$ lifts the one-particle seam contraction $t$ to the complete
  Fock space $\Lambda^\bullet(\mathbb R^{16})$ ($\dim 2^{16}=65536$); by the exterior-power
  spectrum theorem every eigenvalue is a subset product of $\mathrm{spec}(t)$, so all $2^{16}$
  products lie in $[0,1]$ (a contraction $=$ full-cone RP), with eigenvalue-$1$ multiplicity
  $2^8=256$ (wedges of the rank-$8$ $K_\Sigma$ polarisation) and sub-leading $=$ the one-particle
  gap $(2/3)^6$ --- so full-cone RP reduces \emph{for every $m$} (not only $m\le6$, \vref{v161}) to
  the one-particle contraction (Shale--Stinespring), discharging the \vref{v160} scope premise.
  (2) \emph{$A_2$ assembled $+$ verified}: the $(E_8)_1$ character
  $E_4/\eta^8=1+248q+4124q^2+34752q^3+213126q^4+1057504q^5$ (level-$1=248$, extends the order-4
  \vref{v156} check by one order), the embedding $248=120+128$, and the $E_8$ Cartan matrix even
  with $\det 1$ (the unique rank-$8$ even unimodular lattice, \vref{v83}); the net \emph{exists} by
  cited theorems (free-fermion net, lattice VOA, index-$4$ Q-system, \vref{v125}). (3) Both then
  need the \emph{same} input --- the seam realisation \texttt{QGEO.REALIZE.01} (finite half proven,
  \vref{v168}) --- which is a constructive-geometry/AQFT statement, \emph{not} closeable by a finite
  computation, and is left honestly \mO. \textbf{Net:} net existence and full-cone RP become \mE;
  the one irreducible structural premise is the seam realisation. Cited in

\subsection*{2026-06-13 (QGEO rigidity theorem v168 + $\eta_B$ leptogenesis interface v169)}
\begin{itemize}

  \texttt{GATE.QGEO} (the seam $=$ flavour $=$ horizon identification). Exact, machine-checked:
  $\mu_4=\{1,i,-1,-i\}$ has cross-ratio $2$ and a faithful M\"obius stabiliser of order $8=|D_4|$;
  $H^1(\mathbb P^1\!\setminus\!\mu_4)$ has rank $4-1=N_{\mathrm{fam}}=3$; and the forms
  $\omega_k=z^{k-1}dz/(z^4-1)$ ($k=1,2,3$) are $\mu_4$-eigenforms with characters
  $\chi_1,\chi_2,\chi_3$ of weights $(1,2,3)=$ A$_3$ exponents $=\operatorname{Spec}(Q_+)$. So a
  genus-0 boundary with faithful $D_4$, four parabolic marks and this $\mu_4$-decomposition is
  M\"obius-equivalent to $\mathbb P^1\!\setminus\!\mu_4$ --- the QGEO Rigidity Theorem
  (\texttt{QGEO.RIGID.01}, \mE). The seam-collar realisation stays the one premise
  (\texttt{QGEO.REALIZE.01}, \mC). Mirrored in the Wolfram extension (226/226). Cited in
  \texttt{tfpt\_research\_contracts} (U0). \emph{Not} a new structural class --- it hardens the
  existing hinge (consistent with v167's completeness claim).
\item \textbf{\texttt{v169\_etaB\_boltzmann\_interface.py} \mC{} (claim \texttt{FR.ETAB.02}).}
  Operationalises the Tier-3 $F_{\mathrm{transfer}}$ leptogenesis path. Type-I thermal
  leptogenesis $\eta_B\sim0.96\times10^{-2}\varepsilon_1\kappa_f$ (sphaleron $28/79$), fed by
  TFPT's normal-ordered neutrino spectrum and the predicted $\delta_{CP}=240^\circ$. Over natural
  $M_1\in[3\times10^9,3\times10^{10}]$ GeV and washout, $\eta_B$ brackets the observed
  $6.1\times10^{-10}$ (a canonical point gives $6.0\times10^{-10}$, untuned) --- the route is
  \emph{viable}. But $M_1$/washout are scenario inputs, so $\eta_B$ stays \mC; if a precise solve
  excluded the window the leptogenesis \emph{route} falls, not the theory (the downstream
  $\Omega_b$ readout is independent). Cited in \texttt{tfpt\_4\_frontier} (Route B). Python-only.

\subsection*{2026-06-13 (Higgs quartic from the free seam: SM near-criticality explained, v166)}
\begin{itemize}
\item \textbf{\texttt{v166\_higgs\_free\_seam.py} \mE/\mC{} (claim \texttt{HIGGS.FREESEAM.01}).}
  A new prediction tying the Higgs mass to premise~(A). The seam UV is the free chiral
  $c{=}8$ fixed point (v158, Gaussian, no relevant/marginal interactions), so the one
  marginal SM scalar coupling vanishes there: $\lambda(M_{\mathrm{seam}})=0$ and
  $\beta_\lambda(M_{\mathrm{seam}})=0$ --- the Shaposhnikov--Wetterich double-criticality,
  here \emph{derived} from the free seam, not assumed. Integrating the PyR@TE-confirmed
  \emph{two-loop} SM RGEs from $M_Z$ up with the measured $(m_H,m_t)$ gives
  $\lambda(\bar M_{\mathrm{Pl}})\approx0.002$ and $\beta_\lambda(\bar M_{\mathrm{Pl}})\approx0$:
  the famous SM near-criticality is a \emph{consequence} of the free seam (2-loop sharpens
  $\lambda(\bar M_{\mathrm{Pl}})$ from ${\sim}0.022$ at one loop to ${\sim}0.002$). The double
  condition predicts $m_H\sim129$--$134$ GeV; the same condition at the scalaron scale gives
  ${\sim}107$ GeV (too low), so the boundary condition lives at the reduced Planck scale
  (seam $=$ horizon $=$ Planck). Fills the Higgs-sector gap (was only $N_\Phi=1$); cited in
  \texttt{tfpt\_4\_frontier}.
\item PyR@TE-sourced: the reproducer's SM run supplies the two-loop $\beta_\lambda$, reduced
  to top-only (\texttt{verification/pyrate/sm\_higgs\_betas.txt}). Suite now 166 modules.
  Python-only (numerical 2-loop ODE).
\end{itemize}

\subsection*{2026-06-13 (PyR@TE $F_{\mathrm{transfer}}$ follow-ups: flavor scale-tagging v163, QCD scale v164)}
\begin{itemize}
\item \textbf{\texttt{v163\_rg\_stability\_flavor.py} \mE/\mC{} (claim \texttt{FLAV.RGSTAB.01}).}

  ($\sin^2\theta_{12}=\tfrac13-\tfrac{\varphi_0}{2}=0.3067$,

  $|\Delta\sin^2\theta_{ij}|\lesssim10^{-4}$ --- two to three orders below precision.
  Seam value $=$ measured value; the $y_t^2$-driven quark mass ratios ($m_t/m_b\sim41$)
  by contrast carry a scale tag. Cited in \texttt{tfpt\_2} (solar/reactor angle box).

  $\sim0.5$ GeV by dimensional transmutation --- so the QCD-scale \emph{numerator} of

  $m_p/m_e=1836$ stays the honest ``\mO\ --- not forced'' frontier ratio. Cited in

\subsection*{2026-06-13 (PyR@TE external cross-check of the $F_{\mathrm{transfer}}$ gauge inputs --- v159)}

\subsection*{2026-06-13 (the final identification: premise A factors into the already-open A2 + R1, no new open content, \vref{v162})}
\begin{itemize}
\item \textbf{New module \texttt{v162\_seam\_transport\_identification.py} \mE/\mO.} Pushes the \vref{v161}
  residual as far as it rigorously goes and shows it carries \emph{no new open content}. The one-particle
  symbol splits into a gap value $(\beta)$ and a fixed space $(\alpha)$. \textbf{$(\beta)$ is forced:} a
  $\mu_4$-equivariant generator is diagonal in the cusp basis (the deck average is the diagonal projection,
  $\sum_{k}U^kXU^{-k}=|\mu_4|\operatorname{diag}X$ for $U{=}\operatorname{diag}(1,i,-i)$; the commutant of
  $U$ is exactly the diagonal algebra), so its spectrum is the cusp weights
  $\operatorname{spec}(A_0^\star){=}\{0,\tfrac13,\tfrac23\}$ (\vref{v115}) and the transfer eigenvalue
  $(1{-}\alpha)^{p_2}$ with $p_2{=}6{=}|R_+(A_3)|$ gives $\{1,(2/3)^6,(1/3)^6\}$, gap $6\log\tfrac32$ ---
  all carrier data; the lift to the $16$ Majoranas is the $A_3$ subnet grading (\vref{v137}).
  \textbf{$(\alpha)$} is the rank-$8$ Calder\'on polarisation of $\omega_k{=}|k|$ (\vref{v113}/\vref{v156}).
  \textbf{Closure:} with \vref{v160}$+$\vref{v161}, (A) closes given only $\mu_4$-equivariance $+$
  admissibility, whose two non-derived inputs are the already-open A2 (net existence, Kawahigashi--Longo)
  and R1 (seam clock, \texttt{HOR.CLOCK}). So premise~(A) factors exactly into $A_2+R_1$ --- it adds
  \emph{no} independent open item and is closed \emph{conditionally} on them (a unification, not an
  unconditional proof; ledger \texttt{GATE.METRIC.18}). Python-only (numpy/sympy $+$ stdlib).
\item \textbf{Bookkeeping.} Suite at $162$ modules, all green; Wolfram extension unchanged at $224/224$;
  \texttt{tfpt\_research\_contracts} (premise-A keybox) and \texttt{next.txt} moved together.
\end{itemize}

\subsection*{2026-06-13 (the cone reduces to one particle: premise A's scope premise discharged to a 16-dim statement, \vref{v161})}
\begin{itemize}
\item \textbf{New module \texttt{v161\_one\_particle\_reduction.py} \mE/\mO.} \emph{Discharges} the scope
  premise of \vref{v160} (``the transport is gapped on the \emph{full} Schwinger cone'') via Bogoliubov
  second quantisation. A quasi-free transport is $T_\Sigma{=}\Gamma(t)$, the second quantisation of a
  one-particle contraction $t$ on the $16$-dim Majorana space; $\Gamma(t)$ acts on the degree-$m$ correlator
  sector as the exterior power $\Lambda^m(t)$. Machine-checked: (1) $\operatorname{spec}(\Gamma(t)|_{\deg m})
  ={}$ products of $m$ one-particle eigenvalues (compound-matrix theorem, all $m{=}0..6$); (2) \textbf{the
  cone gap equals the one-particle gap} --- the sub-leading eigenvalue over the whole cone is $(2/3)^6$
  exactly, so premise~5 on the cumulant space \emph{is} premise~5 on the $16$-dim space; (3) the
  eigenvalue-$1$ sector is $\Lambda^{*}$ of the fixed subspace (disconnected Wick powers), with uniqueness
  closed by \vref{v113} (one polarisation $\Leftrightarrow$ one vacuum); (4) quasi-freeness is \emph{forced}
  --- the $120{=}\dim\mathfrak{so}(16)$ chiral currents are the Bogoliubov generators and \vref{v158} makes
  every non-Gaussian deformation irrelevant. \textbf{Consequence:} \vref{v160}'s three full-cone premises
  collapse to ONE finite ($16$-dim) one-particle statement (seam symbol $=$ gapped Calder\'on Bogoliubov
  map, fixed $=$ rank-$8$ $K_\Sigma$, gap $(2/3)^6$); all numbers supplied, only the physical identification
  (Kawahigashi--Longo class $=$ the A2 net residual) stays open --- the infinite-dimensional cone is
  eliminated (ledger \texttt{GATE.METRIC.17}). Python-only (numpy $+$ stdlib).
\item \textbf{Bookkeeping.} Suite at $161$ modules, all green; Wolfram extension unchanged at $224/224$;
  \texttt{tfpt\_research\_contracts} (premise-A keybox) and \texttt{next.txt} moved together.

\subsection*{2026-06-13 (premise A as a conditional fixed-point theorem; the load relocates to one scope premise, \vref{v160})}

  and types it honestly. The \emph{exact} parts: (1) a quasi-free state has \emph{all} higher connected

  cumulant inversion on a concrete pure Majorana covariance (the \vref{v113} ``one kernel $=$ net'' property
  at the cumulant level); (2) a kernel-preserving transport fixes the whole quasi-free state by Wick
  functoriality; (3) the Perron--Frobenius dichotomy (a \emph{fixed} $\kappa_{2n}$ is a second fixed ray
  $\Rightarrow$ breaks uniqueness; a \emph{non-fixed} one decays by the gap) forces Gaussianity; (4) the
  qualitative claim needs only $\mathrm{gap}{>}0$, the value $(2/3)^6$ only sets the rate. \textbf{The
  honest residual:} \vref{v56}'s gapped PF uniqueness lives on the \emph{three-dimensional} scalar transfer
  spectrum $\{1,(2/3)^6,(1/3)^6\}$, while the $16$-Majorana seam already carries $\binom{16}{4}{=}1820$ and
  $\binom{16}{6}{=}8008$ higher-cumulant directions --- so (A) reduces to the single internal, exact-testable
  statement ``the admissible TFPT seam transport is primitive $+$ spectrally gapped on the \emph{full}

  establish (ledger \texttt{GATE.METRIC.16}). Python-only (numpy $+$ stdlib); no new exact-identity content

\subsection*{2026-06-13 (premise A: the destination fixed point is provably stable, \vref{v158})}

\item \textbf{The free chiral $c{=}8$ fixed point is provably stable (\vref{v158}, exact dimension count).}
  The finite core of (A)'s ``reaches-the-fixed-point'' residual: the chiral Majorana has $h{=}\tfrac12$,
  the bilinear current $h{=}1$, the quartic $h{=}2$. The relevant window $0<h<1$ for bosonic deformations
  is \emph{empty}, the $h{=}1$ currents are chiral (\vref{v157}, not $(1,1)$-marginal), and the lowest
  interaction (quartic, $h{=}2$) is irrelevant --- so the fixed point is isolated and stable against all
  interactions. Premise (A) reduces to a basin-of-attraction statement with a \emph{proven} stable target
  (ledger \texttt{GATE.METRIC.15}). \emph{Tooling note:} PyR@TE (4d gauge-Yukawa RGEs) is the wrong tool
  for this 2d boundary-CFT residual, but the right tool for the $F_{\mathrm{transfer}}$ interfaces

\subsection*{2026-06-13 (premise A reframed: freeness is a rigid boundary fixed point, \vref{v157})}
\begin{itemize}
\item \textbf{The free-bulk premise becomes a fixed-point property (\vref{v157}, simplicity-first).}
  Instead of postulating Gaussianity, three facts click: (i) the DtN/Calder\'on symbol is
  \emph{universally} $|k|$ (Lee--Uhlmann --- order-$1$ $\Psi$DO, principal symbol $|\xi|_g$;
  interactions live in the irrelevant lower-order symbol), so the free dispersion is
  bulk-detail-independent; (ii) a holomorphic $c{=}8$ theory is \emph{rigid} --- every field has
  $\bar h{=}0$, so no marginal $(1,1)$ field exists and the fixed point is isolated, with no knob for an
  interaction; (iii) the same $|\Z_2|$ that halves $8\pi$ in $\cthree=\tfrac1{8\pi}$ is the Ramond/GSO
  projection giving $\mu{=}1$ ($248{=}120_{\mathrm{NS}}{+}128_{\mathrm R}$). With $(E_8)_1$ unique
  (\vref{v83}), premise~(A) shrinks from ``prove the seam is Gaussian'' to ``the gapped
  ($\Delta{=}6\log\tfrac32$) boundary flow reaches the holomorphic fixed point'' --- freeness then forced
  by rigidity, not fine-tuned (ledger \texttt{GATE.METRIC.14}).

\subsection*{2026-06-13 (external review formalised: No-Unit Theorem + Simple-Current Extension Theorem, \vref{v153}--\vref{v154})}
\begin{itemize}
\item \textbf{$v_{\mathrm{geo}}$ re-typed: the No-Unit Theorem (\vref{v153}).} Every load-bearing
  compiler datum is mass-dimension $0$ and invariant under a unit rescaling $L\mapsto\lambda L$,
  whereas a mass / $1/G$ is not --- so a dimensionless boundary compiler \emph{provably cannot}
  select an absolute scale. $v_{\mathrm{geo}}$ is therefore an \emph{irreducible metrology
  primitive}, not an open gap, and the three apparent residuals collapse onto it
  ($U_{\mathrm{point}}\sim v_{\mathrm{geo}}$, $1/G\sim v_{\mathrm{geo}}^2$, $m/\mu=e^{3/4}$ a pure
  ratio); the irreducibles stay $\{$one unit, $\pi\}$ (ledger \texttt{ANCHOR.VGEO.02}).
\item \textbf{$G_{\mathrm{net}}$ stated as the central closing theorem (\vref{v154}).} The Simple-Current
  Extension Theorem: $A{=}(D_5)_1{\otimes}(A_3)_1$ extended by the isotropic glue
  $L{=}\langle(1,1)\rangle$ has $[B{:}A]{=}|L|{=}4$, $c{=}5{+}3{=}8$,
  $\mu(B){=}\mu(A)/|L|^2{=}16/16{=}1\Rightarrow$ holomorphic $\Rightarrow B\cong(E_8)_1$ ($SO(16)_1$
  excluded). Every algebraic ingredient is machine-checked (\vref{v89}/\vref{v92}/\vref{v125}/%
  \vref{v143}/\vref{v148}); the only residue is the seam-side identification. Pulled to the front of
  \texttt{tfpt\_research\_contracts}, \texttt{tfpt\_5\_redteam} (Target~A final form) and
  \texttt{origin\_theory} (ledger \texttt{GATE.METRIC.11}).
\item \textbf{Status surfaces re-typed} (review): the canonical status card now reads
  $v_{\mathrm{geo}}$ as a metrology \emph{primitive}, $G_{\mathrm{net}}$ as the simple-current
  extension $\cong(E_8)_1$ (\mE/\mC), and $F_{\mathrm{transfer}}$ as one functor with four typed
  interfaces --- ``not structural gaps''. The final one-line framing (dimensionless boundary compiler;
  irreducibles $\{\pi, v_{\mathrm{geo}}\}$; one seam-net theorem; frontier $=$ $F_{\mathrm{transfer}}$)

\item \textbf{Bookkeeping.} Suite at $154$ modules, all green; Wolfram extension $221/221$;

\subsection*{2026-06-12 (R1--R5 second round: every class at its floor, \vref{v145}--\vref{v148})}

  duality), all three pairings become atom arithmetic --- including the \emph{new}

  $\|\sigma\|^2=110=|\Z_2|\gcar\|\mathrm{Pl}(K)\|_1$. R4$'$ $=$ derive \emph{one} map
  (ledger \texttt{GATE.UWALL.13}).
\item \textbf{R5: the M\"obius $D_4$ realisation (\vref{v146}).} The \emph{full}
  dihedral symmetry $\langle z{\mapsto}iz,\,z{\mapsto}1/z\rangle$ of the seam curve acts
  on $H^1$ exactly as the integer model: $\iota^*$ is the exponent duality with parity
  $+1$ on the self-conjugate line ($=T_A$ in the cusp basis, glue-swap parity), and
  $\Sigma$ is the $\delta\iota$ class --- the premise reduces to the module
  identification itself (ledger \texttt{FLAV.QGEO.07}).
\item \textbf{R1: the clock is a Gaussian zero-mode integral, and the bend is
  det$'$-clean (\vref{v147}).} Variance ratio $(1-\alpha)$ (forced by norm $=$ area)
  gives the Born-squared ratio $(1-\alpha)^{p_2}$, the $\ln$ series \emph{is} the
  \vref{v127} ring sum; the two quantum weights share \emph{one} Nariai geometry, so the
  bend $\log_{3/2}3$ carries no determinant correction --- the \vref{v144} obstruction is
  localised to the $\alpha=0$ reference (ledger \texttt{HOR.CLOCK.13}).
\item \textbf{R2: the NS/R sector census (\vref{v148}).} The untwisted (Neveu--Schwarz)
  module carries only the \emph{even} discriminant classes (integer weights), so the odd
  $\mu_4$ simple currents have zero NS support --- they are Ramond modules; the R
  zero-mode module ($256$) splits $128{+}128$ into the odd sectors of the \emph{two}
  Lagrangian glues: choosing the glue \emph{is} choosing the R-projection
  ($248=120_{\mathrm{NS}}{+}128_{\mathrm R}$); the one remaining net statement is
  irreducibly twisted-sector (ledger \texttt{GATE.METRIC.10}). \emph{Correction note
  (same day):} the first version of \vref{v148} graded the Ramond labels by the sum
  $q_D{+}q_A$ (not the glue label) and called that module untwisted; the census was
  rewritten as above --- conclusion unchanged, support corrected, the R-sector sheet
  split is new.
\item \textbf{Bookkeeping.} Suite at $148$ modules, all green; Wolfram extension
  $215/215$ (README $+$ \texttt{GATE.WOLFRAM.02} $+$ website counter in lock-step);
  status surfaces (intro card, \texttt{tfpt\_1}, \texttt{origin\_theory} third update,
  \texttt{next.txt}) moved together.
\end{itemize}

\subsection*{2026-06-12 (external review integrated: $\Lambda$ typing, marker migration, website parity)}
\begin{itemize}

\subsection*{2026-06-12 (R1--R5 attack round: four residual classes sharpened, \vref{v141}--\vref{v144})}
\begin{itemize}
\item \textbf{R5 closed at the discrete level (\vref{v141}, deck selection theorem).} The
  \vref{v140} $\Z_3$ choice is \emph{derived}: the established integer deck $G=T_A\Sigma$
  (\vref{v97}/\vref{v98}) pairs the $Q_+{=}1$ cusp line with the self-conjugate character
  $2$, so only the sheet-twisted assignment $(2,3,1)=\mathrm{chars}(-U)$ survives; the cusp
  exponential $i^{Q_+}$ is excluded (same spectrum, wrong grading pairing). Explicit
  conjugacy constructed; under $k\to-k$ only the established sheet $\Z_2$ flips.
  Consequence: Euler grading $=Q_+\!\circ\rho$. \texttt{GATE.QGEO} keeps only its
  realisation premise --- no discrete freedom left (ledger \texttt{FLAV.QGEO.06}).
\item \textbf{R4$'$ narrowed: three pairings $\to$ two (\vref{v142}, frame integrality).}
  Integer covectors in the $(\mathbf1,a,\sigma)$ dual frame form an index-$11$ sublattice
  ($x-3y+z\equiv0$ mod $11$; the index \emph{is} $\|\mathrm{Pl}(K)\|_1$); with
  $(x,y)=(|\Z_2|,\mathrm{rank}\,E_8)$ the $\sigma$-pairing is forced $\equiv0$ mod $11$,
  and primitivity forces the line parameter even. Cramer reductions for both line pairings
  recorded as restructuring (ledger \texttt{GATE.UWALL.12}).
\item \textbf{R2 realised at the finite Lie level (\vref{v143}, graded Frobenius).} The
  $\Z_4$-graded hull carries exact coset duality ($-C_1=C_3$; Killing pairing nondegenerate
  per $g_k\times g_{-k}$), the glue average is exactly the carrier projector (index $4$),
  and each glue sector is one Weyl orbit (simple currents, fusion $=\mathbb C[\Z_4]$) ---
  the \vref{v125} Q-system realised by the hull; residue $=$ one conformal-net statement
  (ledger \texttt{GATE.METRIC.09}).
\item \textbf{R1's det-ratio step derived in-family (\vref{v144}).} $e_2$-rigidity of the
  traceless SdS cubic gives $r_br_c=1-\Delta^2/3$ exactly; with the \vref{v132} anomaly the
  non-zero-mode determinant ratio is $(1-\Delta^2/3)^{4/3}$ --- no first-order term in the
  horizon split (the \vref{v131} cancellation derived, not assumed); deficit coefficient
  $\tfrac{32}{27}=|\mu_4|(\tfrac23)^3$ (audit). Finite-weight absorption stays \mC\ with the
  $6\to\tfrac{14}3$ obstruction stated sharply (ledger \texttt{HOR.CLOCK.12}).
\item \textbf{R3 attempted, honestly unchanged.} No defensible computation landed for the
  seam-determinant$\to$EH step (\texttt{SEAM.THEOREM.01}); the gate keeps its \mO\ typing
  untouched.
\item \textbf{Wolfram mirror extended} to \vref{v141}--\vref{v144}: extension file now
  $211/211$ (\texttt{GATE.WOLFRAM.02} and the wolfram README updated in lock-step); Python
  suite at $144$ modules, all green.
\end{itemize}

\subsection*{2026-06-12 (sync infrastructure: single-source script index, content maps, one audit)}
\begin{itemize}
\item \textbf{Single-source script index.} The master script$\to$check table
  (\texttt{tex-artefacts/verification.tex}) and the website
  \texttt{ScriptIndex.tsx} are now \emph{generated} from one registry
  (\texttt{script\_registry.csv} $+$ \texttt{script\_clusters.csv} in
  \texttt{verification/}) by \texttt{make\_script\_index.py}; both targets carry a
  generated-file header and are never edited by hand.
\item \textbf{Content maps without splitting the papers.}
  \texttt{verification/make\_docs\_map.py} generates \texttt{docs\_map.csv} (every
  paper section with line range, the \texttt{vN} scripts cited there, a content hash
  and a last-changed date) and \texttt{website\_map.csv} (which website file mentions
  which scripts/documents) --- the machine-readable enumeration of all sync surfaces.
\item \textbf{One sync audit.} \texttt{verification/audit\_sync.py} bundles and
  extends the previous loose shell checks, now in \emph{both} directions: suite
  $\leftrightarrow$ \texttt{run\_all.py} $\leftrightarrow$ registry
  $\leftrightarrow$ ledger; every script cited in a paper \emph{body} (the master
  index alone no longer counts); no stale \texttt{\textbackslash veri}/\texttt{\textbackslash vref}
  targets; every new module mentioned in this changelog; website mirror byte-identical
  (PDFs, scripts, \texttt{release.ts} hashes, version stamps); wolfram counts; overfull
  boxes. Frozen exceptions live in \texttt{audit\_baseline.json} (remove-only).
\item \textbf{Build pipeline.} \texttt{build.sh} gains \texttt{gen} /
  \texttt{website} / \texttt{audit} / \texttt{release} steps; \texttt{notes} now
  regenerates the single-source surfaces first; \texttt{website} copies all active
  PDFs (now incl.\ \texttt{tfpt\_5\_redteam.pdf} and \texttt{changelog.pdf}, with new
  \texttt{release.ts} entries) and the \texttt{vN} scripts, and stamps version, date
  and git revision into \texttt{website/lib/version.ts} (shown in the site header) and
  \texttt{release.ts}.
\item \textbf{Citation gaps closed.} The audit immediately found three scripts cited
  only in the master index: \vref{v17} and \vref{v85} are now cited in their
  \texttt{tfpt\_2} sections (hexagonal resolvent; master cover), and two short
  \texttt{\textbackslash veri\{v19\}} citations were expanded to the full script name.
  \vref{v91} (spine tetrahedron) had no paper section at all --- it is now integrated:
  a keybox in \texttt{tfpt\_3} (``Three views of one spine'': anchor closure, edge/face
  products, volume $120$, $K_6$ negative control, the tautology/sub-grammar caveats) and
  a closing note in the \texttt{tfpt\_1} Spine Quotient Lemma; the
  \texttt{ARCH.SPINE.01} ledger location is corrected to \texttt{tfpt\_1;tfpt\_3} and the
  baseline exception list is empty again.
\item \textbf{Rules.} \texttt{.cursor/rules} updated (\texttt{tfpt-workflow},
  \texttt{website-sync}) and a new \texttt{sync-maps} rule added describing the agentic
  procedure: \emph{regenerate} the maps first, enumerate the affected surfaces from
  them, audit as the exit gate. The mirror map (\texttt{website\_map.csv}) also covers
  the root \texttt{README.md} and \texttt{next.txt} (bare \texttt{vN} ids resolved to
  full script names), and both files are named explicitly as status surfaces that move
  with every finding.
\end{itemize}

\subsection*{2026-06-12 (marker simplification to 4 classes + status reconciliation)}
\begin{itemize}
\item \textbf{Four-class display markers.} The reader-facing marker system is collapsed from eleven
  symbols to four: \mE\ exact / machine-proven (identity, Lie/lattice, formalised, numerical FP),
  \mC\ conditional (physical / bridge / readout under named hypotheses), \mO\ open / axiom, and \mX\
  kill test. \texttt{tex-artefacts/tfpt\_style.tex} defines \texttt{\textbackslash mE/\textbackslash
  mC/\textbackslash mO/\textbackslash mX} and keeps the legacy \texttt{\textbackslash tI \ldots
  \textbackslash tX} names as aliases that render their class. All marker call-sites across the nine
  documents and the shared fragments were rewritten, collapsing same-class combinations (e.g.\
  \texttt{[I]/[L]}\,$\to$\,\mE, \texttt{[N]/[P]}\,$\to$\,\mE/\mC). The fine-grained per-claim type
  (Axiom / Formal / Lattice / Numerical / Identity / Physical) is unchanged in
  \texttt{status\_ledger.csv} --- the single source of truth --- so no fidelity is lost. The marker key,
  badge bar, README marker table and the workflow rule were updated to match.
\item \textbf{Status tables reconciled against the ledger.} The introduction's inflation/$N_\star$ rows
  are made consistent with \vref{v86}/\texttt{COSMO.NSTAR.01}: $r$ and $n_s$ are shown as the frozen
  \emph{bands} over $N_\star\in[50,60]$ with the scalaron-reheating conditional point $N_\star{=}51.4$
  ($n_s{=}0.9611$, $r{=}0.0045$), replacing the stale point values $N_\star{=}55$ (predictions table)
  and $N_\star\simeq57$ (residual card); the closure-ledger inflation row is re-typed \mE\,$\to$\,\mC
  (conditional on $M_{\rm Star}{=}M_{\rm scal}$ $+$ reheating), matching the other two tables and the
  ledger \texttt{[P]} typing.
\end{itemize}

\subsection*{2026-06-12 (later)}
\begin{itemize}
\item \textbf{Shared style and central status artifact.} Two new single-source fragments:
